# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="dfc66-102">Tipos obsoletos no .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dfc66-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="dfc66-103"><a name="introduction"></a>As tabelas deste artigo listam os tipos que estão obsoletos no [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] e no [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organizados por assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dfc66-103"><a name="introduction"></a> The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dfc66-104">Use os links a seguir para ver uma lista dos tipos obsoletos e das alternativas recomendadas em cada assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dfc66-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dfc66-105">Como esses tipos são obsoletos, todos seus membros também estão obsoletos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dfc66-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dfc66-106">Para obter uma lista de membros obsoletos adicionais na biblioteca de classes .NET Framework, confira [Membros obsoletos](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dfc66-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="dfc66-133">Tipos obsoletos em assemblies de sistema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dfc66-133">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="dfc66-134">As tabelas a seguir listam os tipos que foram declarados obsoletos em assemblies de sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dfc66-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dfc66-135">Esses assemblies são usados no desenvolvimento de aplicativos de uso\-geral direcionados ao .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dfc66-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="dfc66-928">Assembly: IEHost.dll e IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dfc66-928">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>
